join-group with new metadata => PREPARING_REBALANCE\n     *             group is removed by partition emigration => DEAD\n     */\n    STABLE(\"Stable\"),\n\n    /**\n     * Group has no more members heartbeat with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\n     *         respond to leave group with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\n     *         respond to offset commit with UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID\n     *         allow offset fetch requests\n     * transition: DEAD is a final state before group metadata is cleaned up, so there are no transitions\n     */\n    DEAD(\"Dead\");\n\n    private final String name;\n    private final String lowerCaseName;\n    private Set<ClassicGroupState> validPreviousStates;\n\n    static {\n        EMPTY.addValidPreviousStates(PREPARING_REBALANCE);\n        PREPARING_REBALANCE.addValidPreviousStates(STABLE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, EMPTY);\n        COMPLETING_REBALANCE.addValidPreviousStates(PREPARING_REBALANCE);\n        STABLE.addValidPreviousStates(COMPLETING_REBALANCE);\n        DEAD.addValidPreviousStates(STABLE, PREPARING_REBALANCE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, EMPTY, DEAD);\n    }\n\n    ClassicGroupState(String name) {\n        this.name = name;\n        this.lowerCaseName = name.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return name;\n    }\n\n    public String toLowerCaseString() {\n        return lowerCaseName;\n    }\n\n    private void addValidPreviousStates(ClassicGroupState... validPreviousStates) {\n        this.validPreviousStates = new HashSet<>(Arrays.asList(validPreviousStates));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @return valid previous states a group must be in to transition to this state.\n     */\n    public Set<ClassicGroupState> The core components include:\\n\\n## Core Coordinator Interface and Services\\n\\n1. **GroupCoordinator.java** - Defines the main interface with methods for joinGroup(), syncGroup(), heartbeat() for classic groups, and consumerGroupHeartbeat(), streamsGroupHeartbeat(), shareGroupHeartbeat() for modern group protocols.\\n\\n2. **GroupCoordinatorService.java** - Implements GroupCoordinator interface, orchestrating request routing and response handling for all group types. Contains public methods: joinGroup() at line 846, syncGroup() at line 900, heartbeat() at line 944.\\n\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** - Implements CoordinatorShard interface, managing per-shard state and coordinating with GroupMetadataManager for actual state machine transitions.\\n\\n## State Machine Implementation (Classic Groups)\\n\\n4. **ClassicGroupState.java** - Defines the classic group state machine enum with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: Group with no members, lingers until offsets expire\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group preparing to rebalance, members joining\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group awaiting state assignment from leader\\n   - STABLE: Group is stable, normal operation\\n   - DEAD: Group metadata being removed\\n   The state transitions are strictly defined with validPreviousStates() method.\\n\\n5. **ClassicGroup.java** - Holds metadata for classic groups where member assignment is driven from client side. Implements state transitions using transitionTo() method and manages member collection.\\n\\n## Member and Heartbeat Management\\n\\n6. **ClassicGroupMember.java** - Represents group members with heartbeat session management. Key methods include:\\n   - hasSatisfiedHeartbeat(): Checks if member's heartbeat expectation is satisfied (line 207)\\n   - sessionTimeoutMs(): Returns session timeout (line 306)\\n   - Tracks latest heartbeat timestamp and session timeout for expiry detection\\n\\n7. **GroupMetadataManager.java** - Central state machine manager handling all group types and request processing. Contains methods for:\\n   - ClassicGroupJoinGroup: Processes JoinGroup requests, manages state transitions from EMPTY/STABLE to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n   - ClassicGroupSyncGroup: Processes SyncGroup requests, transitions from PREPARING_REBALANCE to COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE\\n   - ClassicGroupHeartbeat: Processes Heartbeat requests, detects member failures via hasSatisfiedHeartbeat()\\n   - Session timeout scheduling via scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout()\\n\\n## Modern Group Types\\n\\n8. **ModernGroup.java** - Base class for modern protocol groups\\n9. **ModernGroupMember.java** - Base member class for modern groups\\n10. **ConsumerGroup.java** - Implementation for new consumer group protocol with heartbeat-based member lifecycle\\n11. **ConsumerGroupMember.java** - Consumer group members with ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData handling\\n12. **StreamsGroup.java** - Streams groups supporting streams topology coordination\\n13. **StreamsGroupMember.java** - Streams group members with topology-aware heartbeats\\n14. **ShareGroup.java** - Share group implementation for shared consumption\\n15. **ShareGroupMember.java** - Share group members\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n16. **Group.java** - Common interface for all group types\\n17. **GroupConfig.java** - When heartbeats are not satisfied, members are marked for removal and trigger transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE state.\\n\\nFor modern group protocols, ConsumerGroupHeartbeat requests (GroupCoordinatorService.consumerGroupHeartbeat()) manage member lifecycle with similar expiry detection mechanisms, as do StreamsGroupHeartbeat and ShareGroupHeartbeat methods.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1704,"cache_read_input_tokens":52307,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1704},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b1551a8a-f3e7-4cc6-b79f-e5ee4ff14122","uuid":"7fda2964-baeb-4bbb-ba89-9edebef8ff03"}

The core components include:\\n\\n## Core Coordinator Interface and Services\\n\\n1. **GroupCoordinator.java** - Defines the main interface with methods for joinGroup(), syncGroup(), heartbeat() for classic groups, and consumerGroupHeartbeat(), streamsGroupHeartbeat(), shareGroupHeartbeat() for modern group protocols.\\n\\n2. **GroupCoordinatorService.java** - Implements GroupCoordinator interface, orchestrating request routing and response handling for all group types. Contains public methods: joinGroup() at line 846, syncGroup() at line 900, heartbeat() at line 944.\\n\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** - Implements CoordinatorShard interface, managing per-shard state and coordinating with GroupMetadataManager for actual state machine transitions.\\n\\n## State Machine Implementation (Classic Groups)\\n\\n4. **ClassicGroupState.java** - Defines the classic group state machine enum with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: Group with no members, lingers until offsets expire\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group preparing to rebalance, members joining\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group awaiting state assignment from leader\\n   - STABLE: Group is stable, normal operation\\n   - DEAD: Group metadata being removed\\n   The state transitions are strictly defined with validPreviousStates() method.\\n\\n5. **ClassicGroup.java** - Holds metadata for classic groups where member assignment is driven from client side. Implements state transitions using transitionTo() method and manages member collection.\\n\\n## Member and Heartbeat Management\\n\\n6. **ClassicGroupMember.java** - Represents group members with heartbeat session management. Key methods include:\\n   - hasSatisfiedHeartbeat(): Checks if member's heartbeat expectation is satisfied (line 207)\\n   - sessionTimeoutMs(): Returns session timeout (line 306)\\n   - Tracks latest heartbeat timestamp and session timeout for expiry detection\\n\\n7. **GroupMetadataManager.java** - Central state machine manager handling all group types and request processing. Contains methods for:\\n   - ClassicGroupJoinGroup: Processes JoinGroup requests, manages state transitions from EMPTY/STABLE to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n   - ClassicGroupSyncGroup: Processes SyncGroup requests, transitions from PREPARING_REBALANCE to COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE\\n   - ClassicGroupHeartbeat: Processes Heartbeat requests, detects member failures via hasSatisfiedHeartbeat()\\n   - Session timeout scheduling via scheduleConsumerGroupSessionTimeout()\\n\\n## Modern Group Types\\n\\n8. **ModernGroup.java** - Base class for modern protocol groups\\n9. **ModernGroupMember.java** - Base member class for modern groups\\n10. **ConsumerGroup.java** - Implementation for new consumer group protocol with heartbeat-based member lifecycle\\n11. **ConsumerGroupMember.java** - Consumer group members with ConsumerGroupHeartbeatRequestData handling\\n12. **StreamsGroup.java** - Streams groups supporting streams topology coordination\\n13. **StreamsGroupMember.java** - Streams group members with topology-aware heartbeats\\n14. **ShareGroup.java** - Share group implementation for shared consumption\\n15. **ShareGroupMember.java** - Share group members\\n\\n## Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n16. **Group.java** - Common interface for all group types\\n17. **GroupConfig.java** - Configuration management for group behavior\\n18. **GroupCoordinatorConfig.java** - Coordinator-level configuration\\n19. **GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java** - Helpers for record serialization with sessionTimeout handling\\n20. **GroupCoordinatorRecordSerde.java** - When heartbeats are not satisfied, members are marked for removal and trigger transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE state.\\n\\nFor modern group protocols, ConsumerGroupHeartbeat requests (GroupCoordinatorService.consumerGroupHeartbeat()) manage member lifecycle with similar expiry detection mechanisms, as do StreamsGroupHeartbeat and ShareGroupHeartbeat methods.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
